MING, 'GA' ZHIG GANG GI RJES SU 'BRANG BA'I SLOB DPON GYI SGO
NAS MING BTAGS PA YIN TE, DE NYID LAS, YUL DON SLOB DPON BYE
BRAG GIS, ,THA DAD RNAM PA BCO BRGYAD GSUNGS, ZHES GSUNGS PA'I
PHYIR, GNYIS PA BKA' BSDU MDZAD TSUL DNGOS NI, STON PA MYA NGAN

MDZAD NAS, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' LNGA BRGYA, DGRA BCOM PA LNGA

PAS,
